}\n136\t}\n137\t\n138\t/// Build router for document endpoints.\n139\tpub fn router<S>() -> Router<S>\n140\twhere\n141\t    S: Clone + Send + Sync + 'static,\n142\t{\n143\t    Router::new()\n144\t        .route(\"/\", axum::routing::post(post_documents))\n145\t        .route(\"/\", axum::routing::put(put_documents))\n146\t        .route(\"/\", axum::routing::delete(delete_documents))\n147\t        .route(\"/:id\", axum::routing::delete(delete_document_by_id))\n148\t}\n149\t\n150\t/// POST /indexes/{uid}/documents - Add documents.\n151\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %index))]\n152\tasync fn post_documents(\n153\t    Path(index): Path<String>,\n154\t    Query(params): Query<DocumentsParams>,\n155\t    Extension(state): Extension<Arc<AppState>>,\n156\t    session_id: Option<Extension<crate::middleware::SessionId>>,\n157\t    Json(documents): Json<Vec<Value>>,\n158\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n159\t    // Extract session ID from request extensions (set by session_pinning_middleware)\n160\t    let sid = session_id.and_then(|ext| {\n161\t        let s = ext.0;\n162\t        if s.0.is_empty() { None } else { Some(s.0.clone()) }\n163\t    });\n164\t\n165\t    write_documents_impl(index, params.primaryKey, documents, &state, sid).await\n166\t}\n167\t\n168\t/// PUT /indexes/{uid}/documents - Replace documents.\n169\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %index))]\n170\tasync fn put_documents(\n171\t    Path(index): Path<String>,\n172\t    Query(params): Query<DocumentsParams>,\n173\t    Extension(state): Extension<Arc<AppState>>,\n174\t    session_id: Option<Extension<crate::middleware::SessionId>>,\n175\t    Json(documents): Json<Vec<Value>>,\n176\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n177\t    let sid = session_id.and_then(|ext| {\n178\t        let s = ext.0;\n179\t        if s.0.is_empty() { None } else { Some(s.0.clone()) }\n180\t    });\n181\t    write_documents_impl(index, params.primaryKey, documents, &state, sid).await\n182\t}\n183\t\n184\t/// DELETE /indexes/{uid}/documents - Delete by IDs or filter.\n185\tasync fn delete_documents(\n186\t    Path(index): Path<String>,\n187\t    Extension(state): Extension<Arc<AppState>>,\n188\t    session_id: Option<Extension<crate::middleware::SessionId>>,\n189\t    Json(body): Json<Value>,\n190\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n191\t    let sid = session_id.and_then(|ext| {\n192\t        let s = ext.0;\n193\t        if s.0.is_empty() { None } else { Some(s.0.clone()) }\n194\t    });\n195\t\n196\t    // Try to parse as delete by filter first\n197\t    if let Some(filter) = body.get(\"filter\") {\n198\t        let req = DeleteByFilterRequest {\n199\t            index_uid: index.clone(),\n200\t            filter: filter.clone(),\n201\t            origin: None, // Client write\n202\t        };\n203\t        return delete_by_filter_impl(index, req, &state, sid).await;\n204\t    }\n205\t\n206\t    // Try to parse as delete by IDs\n207\t    if let Some(ids) = body.get(\"ids\").and_then(|v| v.as_array()) {\n208\t        let ids: Vec<String> = ids\n209\t            .iter()\n210\t            .filter_map(|v| v.as_str().map(|s| s.to_string()))\n211\t            .collect();\n212\t        if !ids.is_empty() {\n213\t            let req = DeleteByIdsRequest {\n214\t                index_uid: index.clone(),\n215\t                ids,\n216\t                origin: None, // Client write\n217\t            };\n218\t            return delete_by_ids_impl(index, req, &state, sid).await;\n219\t        }\n220\t    }\n221\t\n222\t    // If we get here, the request body is malformed\n223\t    Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n224\t        MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n225\t        \"delete request must include either 'filter' or 'ids' field\",\n226\t    ))\n227\t}\n228\t\n229\t/// DELETE /indexes/{uid}/documents/{id} - Delete single document by ID.\n230\tasync fn delete_document_by_id(\n231\t    Path((index, id)): Path<(String, String)>,\n232\t    Extension(state): Extension<Arc<AppState>>,\n233\t    session_id: Option<Extension<crate::middleware::SessionId>>,\n234\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n235\t    let sid = session_id.and_then(|ext| {\n236\t        let s = ext.0;\n237\t        if s.0.is_empty() { None } else { Some(s.0.clone()) }\n238\t    });\n239\t    let req = DeleteByIdsRequest {\n240\t        index_uid: index.clone(),\n241\t        ids: vec![id],\n242\t        origin: None, // Client write\n243\t    };\n244\t    delete_by_ids_impl(index, req, &state, sid).await\n245\t}\n246\t\n247\t/// Implementation for write documents (POST/PUT).\n248\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %index, session_id))]\n249\tasync fn write_documents_impl(\n250\t    index: String,\n251\t    primary_key: Option<String>,\n252\t    mut documents: Vec<Value>,\n253\t    state: &AppState,\n254\t    session_id: Option<String>,\n255\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n256\t    if documents.is_empty() {\n257\t        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n258\t            MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n259\t            \"cannot write empty document batch\",\n260\t        ));\n261\t    }\n262\t\n263\t    // 1. Resolve alias to concrete index UID (plan §13.7)\n264\t    // Aliases are resolved before any processing; writes to multi-target aliases are rejected\n265\t    let index_uid = if state.config.aliases.enabled {\n266\t        // Check if the index is an alias\n267\t        let resolved = state.alias_registry.resolve(&index).await;\n268\t        if resolved != vec![index.clone()] {\n269\t            // It was an alias\n270\t            // Check if it's a multi-target alias (read-only, ILM-managed)\n271\t            if state.alias_registry.is_multi_target_alias(&index).await {\n272\t                return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n273\t                    MiroirCode::MultiAliasNotWritable,\n274\t                    format!(\n275\t                        \"alias '{}' is a multi-target alias and is read-only (managed by ILM); writes must go to the concrete index or the write alias\",\n276\t                        index\n277\t                    ),\n278\t                ));\n279\t            }\n280\t            // Single-target alias: record resolution metric and use the target\n281\t            state.metrics.inc_alias_resolution(&index);\n282\t            resolved.into_iter().next().unwrap_or_else(|| index.clone())\n283\t        } else {\n284\t            // Not an alias, use the index name as-is\n285\t            index.clone()\n286\t        }\n287\t    } else {\n288\t        index.clone()\n289\t    };\n290\t\n291\t    // 1. Extract primary key from first document if not provided\n292\t    let primary_key = primary_key.or_else(|| {\n293\t        documents\n294\t            .first()\n295\t            .and_then(|doc| extract_primary_key(doc))\n296\t    });\n297\t\n298\t    let primary_key = primary_key.ok_or_else(|| {\n299\t        MeilisearchError::new(\n300\t            MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n301\t            format!(\"primary key required for index `{}`\", index),\n302\t        )\n303\t    })?;\n304\t\n305\t    // 2. Validate all documents have the primary key and check for reserved field\n306\t    let anti_entropy_enabled = state.config.anti_entropy.enabled;\n307\t    let updated_at_field = &state.config.anti_entropy.updated_at_field;\n308\t    let ttl_enabled = state.config.ttl.enabled;\n309\t    let expires_at_field = &state.config.ttl.expires_at_field;\n310\t\n311\t    for (i, doc) in documents.iter().enumerate() {\n312\t        // Check for reserved field BEFORE checking primary key (per acceptance criteria)\n313\t        // _miroir_shard is ALWAYS reserved (plan §5)\n314\t        if doc.get(\"_miroir_shard\").is_some() {\n315\t            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n316\t                MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n317\t                \"document contains reserved field `_miroir_shard`\",\n318\t            ));\n319\t        }\n320\t\n321\t        // _miroir_updated_at is reserved ONLY when anti_entropy.enabled: true (plan §5, §13.8)\n322\t        if anti_entropy_enabled && doc.get(updated_at_field).is_some() {\n323\t            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n324\t                MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n325\t                format!(\"document contains reserved field `{}` (reserved when anti_entropy.enabled: true)\", updated_at_field),\n326\t            ));\n327\t        }\n328\t\n329\t        // _miroir_expires_at is reserved ONLY when ttl.enabled: true (plan §5, §13.14)\n330\t        // When reserved, clients cannot SET it; the orchestrator controls it. When disabled,\n331\t        // client values pass through end-to-end.\n332\t        if ttl_enabled && doc.get(expires_at_field).is_some() {\n333\t            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n334\t                MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n335\t                format!(\"document contains reserved field `{}` (reserved when ttl.enabled: true)\", expires_at_field),\n336\t            ));\n337\t        }\n338\t\n339\t        if doc.get(&primary_key).is_none() {\n340\t            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n341\t                MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n342\t                format!(\n343\t                    \"document at index {} missing primary key field `{}`\",\n344\t                    i, primary_key\n345\t                ),\n346\t            ));\n347\t        }\n348\t    }\n349\t\n350\t    // 3. Inject _miroir_shard and _miroir_updated_at into each document\n351\t    let topology = state.topology.read().await;\n352\t    let shard_count = topology.shards;\n353\t    let rf = topology.rf();\n354\t    let replica_group_count = topology.replica_group_count();\n355\t\n356\t    // Get current timestamp in milliseconds since epoch for _miroir_updated_at stamping\n357\t    let now_ms = if anti_entropy_enabled {\n358\t        Some(\n359\t            std::time::SystemTime::now()\n360\t                .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)\n361\t                .unwrap_or_default()\n362\t                .as_millis() as u64\n363\t        )\n364\t    } else {\n365\t        None\n366\t    };\n367\t\n368\t    for doc in &mut documents {\n369\t        if let Some(pk_value) = doc.get(&primary_key).and_then(|v| v.as_str()) {\n370\t            let shard_id = shard_for_key(pk_value, shard_count);\n371\t            doc[\"_miroir_shard\"] = serde_json::json!(shard_id);\n372\t        }\n373\t\n374\t        // Stamp _miroir_updated_at when anti_entropy is enabled (plan §13.8)\n375\t        // This happens AFTER reserved field validation, so orchestrator-controlled injection is allowed\n376\t        if let Some(timestamp) = now_ms {\n377\t            doc[updated_at_field] = serde_json::json!(timestamp);\n378\t        }\n379\t    }\n380\t\n381\t    // 4. Group documents by target nodes (per-batch grouping for efficient fan-out)\n382\t    let node_documents = group_documents_by_shard(&documents, &primary_key, &topology)?;\n383\t\n384\t    // 5. Fan out to nodes and track quorum\n385\t    let client = HttpClient::new(\n386\t        state.config.node_master_key.clone(),\n387\t        state.config.scatter.node_timeout_ms,\n388\t    );\n389\t\n390\t    let mut quorum_state = QuorumState::default();\n391\t    let mut node_task_uids: HashMap<String, u64> = HashMap::new();\n392\t\n393\t    // For each shard, write to all RF nodes in each replica group (with dual-write support)\n394\t    for (shard_id, docs) in node_documents {\n395\t        // Get migration coordinator reference for dual-write detection\n396\t        let migration_coordinator = state.migration_coordinator.as_ref().map(|c| {\n397\t            // We need a read lock on the coordinator\n398\t            tokio::task::block_in_place(|| {\n399\t                tokio::runtime::Handle::current().block_on(async {\n400\t                    c.read().await\n401\t                })\n402\t            })\n403\t        });\n404\t\n405\t        // Use migration-aware routing\n406\t        let targets = write_targets_with_migration(\n407\t            shard_id,\n408\t            &topology,\n409\t            migration_coordinator.as_deref(),\n410\t        );\n411\t\n412\t        if targets.is_empty() {\n413\t            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n414\t                MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n415\t                format!(\"no available nodes for shard {}\", shard_id),\n416\t            ));\n417\t        }\n418\t\n419\t        // Track which groups we're targeting for this shard\n420\t\n421\t        for node_id in targets {\n422\t            let node = topology\n423\t                .node(&node_id)\n424\t                .ok_or_else(|| MeilisearchError::new(MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable, \"node not found in topology\"))?;\n425\t\n426\t            let group_id = node.replica_group;\n427\t            quorum_state.record_attempt(group_id, &node_id);\n428\t\n429\t            let req = WriteRequest {\n430\t                index_uid: index_uid.clone(),\n431\t                documents: docs.clone(),\n432\t                primary_key: Some(primary_key.clone()),\n433\t                origin: None, // Client write\n434\t            };\n435\t\n436\t            match client.write_documents(&node_id, &node.address, &req).await {\n437\t                Ok(resp) if resp.success => {\n438\t                    quorum_state.record_success(group_id, &node_id);\n439\t                    if let Some(task_uid) = resp.task_uid {\n440\t                        node_task_uids.insert(node_id.as_str().to_string(), task_uid);\n441\t                    }\n442\t                }\n443\t                Ok(resp) => {\n444\t                    // Non-success response (validation error, etc.)\n445\t                    return Ok(build_json_error_response(build_error_response(resp)));\n446\t                }\n447\t                Err(_) => {\n448\t                    quorum_state.record_failure(group_id);\n449\t                }\n450\t            }\n451\t        }\n452\t    }\n453\t\n454\t    // 6. Apply two-rule quorum logic\n455\t    let degraded_groups = quorum_state.count_degraded_groups(replica_group_count, rf);\n456\t    let quorum_groups = quorum_state.count_quorum_groups();\n457\t\n458\t    // Write success if at least one group met quorum\n459\t    if quorum_groups == 0 {\n460\t        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n461\t            MiroirCode::NoQuorum,\n462\t            \"no replica group met quorum\",\n463\t        ));\n464\t    }\n465\t\n466\t    // 6.5. Find the first group to reach quorum (for session pinning, plan §13.6)\n467\t    // Groups are checked in ascending order, so the first one with quorum is the first\n468\t    let first_quorum_group = (0..replica_group_count)\n469\t        .find(|&group_id| {\n470\t            let acks = *quorum_state.group_acks.get(&group_id).unwrap_or(&0);\n471\t            let quorum = (rf / 2) + 1;\n472\t            acks >= quorum\n473\t        })\n474\t        .unwrap_or(0); // Default to group 0 if somehow no quorum (shouldn't happen here)\n475\t\n476\t    // 7. Register Miroir task with collected node task UIDs\n477\t    let miroir_task = state\n478\t        .task_registry\n479\t        .register_with_metadata(\n480\t            node_task_uids.clone(),\n481\t            Some(index_uid.clone()),\n482\t            Some(\"documentAdditionOrUpdate\".to_string()),\n483\t        )\n484\t        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n485\t            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n486\t            format!(\"failed to register task: {}\", e),\n487\t        ))?;\n488\t\n489\t    // 7.5. Record session pinning if session header present (plan §13.6)\n490\t    if let (Some(ref sid), true) = (&session_id, state.session_manager.is_enabled()) {\n491\t        if let Err(e) = state.session_manager.record_write_with_quorum(\n492\t            sid,\n493\t            miroir_task.miroir_id.clone(),\n494\t            first_quorum_group,\n495\t        ).await {\n496\t            // Log error but don't fail the write - session pinning is best-effort\n497\t            tracing::error!(\n498\t                session_id = %sid,\n499\t                error = %e,\n500\t                \"failed to record session pinning for write\"\n501\t            );\n502\t        }\n503\t    }\n504\t\n505\t    // Build success response with degraded header and mtask ID\n506\t    build_response_with_degraded_header(\n507\t        DocumentsWriteResponse {\n508\t            taskUid: Some(miroir_task.miroir_id),\n509\t            indexUid: Some(index_uid.clone()),\n510\t            status: Some(\"enqueued\".to_string()),\n511\t            error: None,\n512\t            error_type: None,\n513\t            code: None,\n514\t            link: None,\n515\t        },\n516\t        degraded_groups,\n517\t    )\n518\t}\n519\t\n520\t/// Implementation for delete by IDs.\n521\tasync fn delete_by_ids_impl(\n522\t    index: String,\n523\t    req: DeleteByIdsRequest,\n524\t    state: &AppState,\n525\t    session_id: Option<String>,\n526\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n527\t    if req.ids.is_empty() {\n528\t        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n529\t            MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n530\t            \"cannot delete empty ID list\",\n531\t        ));\n532\t    }\n533\t\n534\t    // Resolve alias to concrete index UID (plan §13.7)\n535\t    let index_uid = if state.config.aliases.enabled {\n536\t        let resolved = state.alias_registry.resolve(&index).await;\n537\t        if resolved != vec![index.clone()] {\n538\t            // It was an alias - check if it's a multi-target alias (read-only)\n539\t            if state.alias_registry.is_multi_target_alias(&index).await {\n540\t                return }\n548\t            // Single-target alias: record resolution metric and use the target\n549\t            state.metrics.inc_alias_resolution(&index);\n550\t            resolved.into_iter().next().unwrap_or_else(|| index.clone())\n551\t        } else {\n552\t            index.clone()\n553\t        }\n554\t    } else {\n555\t        index.clone()\n556\t    };\n557\t\n558\t    let topology = state.topology.read().await;\n559\t    let rf = topology.rf();\n560\t    let replica_group_count = topology.replica_group_count();\n561\t\n562\t    // Group IDs by state.config.node_master_key.clone(),\n571\t        state.config.scatter.node_timeout_ms,\n572\t    );\n573\t\n574\t    let mut quorum_state = QuorumState::default();\n575\t    let mut node_task_uids: MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n584\t                format!(\"no available nodes for shard {}\", shard_id),\n585\t            ));\n586\t        }\n587\t\n588\t        for node_id in targets {\n589\t topology\"))?;\n592\t\n593\t            let group_id = node.replica_group;\n594\t            quorum_state.record_attempt(group_id, &node_id);\n595\t\n596\t            let delete_req =           match client.delete_documents(&node_id, &node.address, &delete_req).await {\n603\t                Ok(resp) if resp.success => {\n604\t                    quorum_state.record_success(group_id, &node_id);\n605\t                    if let Some(task_uid) = resp.task_uid {\n606\t                        node_task_uids.insert(node_id.as_str().to_string(), task_uid);\n607\t                    }\n608\t                }\n609\t                Ok(resp) => {\n610\t                    return Ok(build_json_error_response(build_error_response(resp)));\n611\t                }\n612\t                Err(_) => {\n613\t                    quorum_state.record_failure(group_id);\n614\t                }\n615\t            }\n616\t        }\n617\t    }\n618\t\n619\t quorum_state.count_quorum_groups();\n622\t\n623\t    // Write success if at least one group met quorum\n624\t    if quorum_groups == 0 {\n625\t        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n626\t            MiroirCode::NoQuorum,\n627\t            \"no replica group met quorum\",\n628\t        ));\n629\t    }\n630\t\n631\t    // Find the first group to reach quorum (for session pinning, plan   let quorum = (rf / 2) + 1;\n636\t            acks >= quorum\n637\t        })\n638\t        .unwrap_or(0);\n639\t\n640\t    // Register Miroir task with collected node task UIDs\n641\t    let Some(\"documentDeletion\".to_string()),\n647\t        )\n648\t        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n649\t            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n650\t            format!(\"failed to register      first_quorum_group,\n659\t        ).await {\n660\t            tracing::error!(\n661\t                session_id = %sid,\n662\t                error = %e,\n663\t                \"failed to record None,\n675\t            code: None,\n676\t            link: None,\n677\t        },\n678\t        degraded_groups,\n679\t    )\n680\t}\n681\t\n682\t/// Implementation for delete by filter (broadcast to all nodes).\n683\tasync fn delete_by_filter_impl(\n684\t    index: String,\n685\t    req: DeleteByFilterRequest,\n686\t    state: &AppState,\n687\t    session_id: Option<String>,\n688\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n689\t    let topology = state.topology.read().await;\n690\t    let rf = topology.rf();\n691\t    let replica_group_count = topology.replica_group_count();\n692\t\n693\t    let client = HttpClient::new(\n694\t        state.config.node_master_key.clone(),\n695\t        state.config.scatter.node_timeout_ms,\n696\t    );\n697\t\n698\t    let mut quorum_state = QuorumState::default();\n699\t    let mut node_task_uids: HashMap<String, u64> = HashMap::new();\n700\t\n701\t    // Broadcast to all nodes (cannot shard-route for filters)\n702\t    for node in topology.nodes() {\n703\t        let group_id = node.replica_group;\n704\t        quorum_state.record_attempt(group_id, &node.id);\n705\t\n706\t        match client\n707\t            .delete_documents_by_filter(&node.id, &node.address, &req)\n708\t            .await\n709\t        {\n710\t            Ok(resp) if resp.success => {\n711\t                quorum_state.record_success(group_id, &node.id);\n712\t                if let Some(task_uid) = resp.task_uid {\n713\t                    node_task_uids.insert(node.id.as_str().to_string(), task_uid);\n714\t                }\n715\t            }\n716\t            Ok(resp) => {\n717\t                return Ok(build_json_error_response(build_error_response(resp)));\n718\t            }\n719\t            Err(_) => {\n720\t                quorum_state.record_failure(group_id);\n721\t            }\n722\t        }\n723\t    }\n724\t\n725\t    // Apply two-rule quorum logic\n726\t    let degraded_groups = quorum_state.count_degraded_groups(replica_group_count, rf);\n727\t    let quorum_groups = quorum_state.count_quorum_groups();\n728\t\n729\t    // Write success if at least one group met quorum\n730\t    if quorum_groups == 0 {\n731\t        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n732\t            MiroirCode::NoQuorum,\n733\t            \"no replica group met quorum\",\n734\t        ));\n735\t    }\n736\t\n737\t    // Find the first group to reach quorum (for session pinning, plan §13.6)\n738\t    let first_quorum_group = (0..replica_group_count)\n739\t        .find(|&group_id| {\n740\t            let acks = *quorum_state.group_acks.get(&group_id).unwrap_or(&0);\n741\t            let quorum = (rf / 2) + 1;\n742\t            acks >= quorum\n743\t        })\n744\t        .unwrap_or(0);\n745\t\n746\t    // Register Miroir task with collected node task UIDs\n747\t    let miroir_task = state\n748\t        .task_registry\n749\t        .register_with_metadata(\n750\t            node_task_uids.clone(),\n751\t            Some(index.clone()),\n752\t            Some(\"documentDeletion\".to_string()),\n753\t        )\n754\t        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n755\t            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n756\t            format!(\"failed to register task: {}\", e),\n757\t        ))?;\n758\t\n759\t    // Record session pinning if session header present (plan §13.6)\n760\t    if let (Some(ref sid), true) = (&session_id, state.session_manager.is_enabled()) {\n761\t        if let Err(e) = state.session_manager.record_write_with_quorum(\n762\t            sid,\n763\t            miroir_task.miroir_id.clone(),\n764\t            first_quorum_group,\n765\t        ).await {\n766\t            tracing::error!(\n767\t                session_id = %sid,\n768\t                error = %e,\n769\t                \"failed to record session pinning for delete by filter\"\n770\t            );\n771\t        }\n772\t    }\n773\t\n774\t    build_response_with_degraded_header(\n775\t        DocumentsWriteResponse {\n776\t            taskUid: Some(miroir_task.miroir_id),\n777\t            indexUid: Some(index.clone()),\n778\t            status: Some(\"enqueued\".to_string()),\n779\t            error: None,\n780\t            error_type: None,\n781\t            code: None,\n782\t            link: None,\n783\t        },\n784\t        degraded_groups,\n785\t    )\n786\t}\n787\t\n788\t/// Extract primary key from a document by checking common field names.\n789\t///\n790\t/// Tries fields in order: id, pk, key, _id.\n791\tfn extract_primary_key(doc: &Value) -> Option<String> {\n792\t    [\"id\", \"pk\", \"key\", \"_id\"]\n793\t        .iter()\n794\t        .find(|&&key| doc.get(key).is_some())\n795\t        .map(|&s| s.to_string())\n796\t}\n797\t\n798\t/// Group documents by their target shard for fan-out optimization.\n799\t///\n800\t/// Returns a map of shard_id -> documents to send to that shard.\n801\t/// The caller then fans out each shard's documents to all RF nodes in each group.\n802\t///\n803\t/// This per-batch grouping minimizes HTTP fan-out count (critical at scale).\n804\tfn group_documents_by_shard(\n805\t    documents: &[Value],\n806\t    primary_key: &str,\n807\t    topology: &Topology,\n808\t) -> std::result::Result<HashMap<u32, Vec<Value>>, MeilisearchError> {\n809\t    let mut shard_documents: HashMap<u32, Vec<Value>> = HashMap::new();\n810\t\n811\t    for doc in documents {\n812\t        let pk_value = doc\n813\t            .get(primary_key)\n814\t            .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n815\t            .ok_or_else(|| {\n816\t                MeilisearchError::new(\n817\t                    MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n818\t                    \"primary key value must be a string\",\n819\t                )\n820\t            })?;\n821\t\n822\t        let shard_id = shard_for_key(pk_value, topology.shards);\n823\t        shard_documents\n824\t            .entry(shard_id)\n825\t            .or_default()\n826\t            .push(doc.clone());\n827\t    }\n828\t\n829\t    Ok(shard_documents)\n830\t}\n831\t\n832\t/// Build an error response from a node error.\n833\tfn build_error_response(resp: WriteResponse) -> DocumentsWriteResponse {\n834\t    DocumentsWriteResponse {\n835\t        taskUid: resp.task_uid.map(|uid| uid.to_string()),\n836\t        indexUid: None,\n837\t        status: None,\n838\t        error: resp.message,\n839\t        error_type: resp.error_type,\n840\t        code: resp.code,\n841\t        link: None,\n842\t    }\n843\t}\n844\t\n845\t/// Build a success response with optional X-Miroir-Degraded header.\n846\tfn build_response_with_degraded_header(\n847\t    response: DocumentsWriteResponse,\n848\t    degraded_groups: u32,\n849\t) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n850\t    let body = serde_json::to_string(&response).map_err(|e| {\n851\t        MeilisearchError::new(\n852\t            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n853\t            format!(\"failed to serialize response: {}\", e),\n854\t        )\n855\t    })?;\n856\t\n857\t    let mut builder = Response::builder()\n858\t        .status(StatusCode::OK)\n859\t        .header(header::CONTENT_TYPE, \"application/json\");\n860\t\n861\t    // Add X-Miroir-Degraded header if any groups were degraded\n862\t    if degraded_groups > 0 {\n863\t        builder = builder.header(HEADER_MIROIR_DEGRADED, format!(\"groups={}\", degraded_groups));\n864\t    }\n865\t\n866\t    Ok(builder\n867\t        .body(axum::body::Body::from(body))\n868\t        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n869\t            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n870\t            format!(\"failed to build response: {}\", e),\n871\t        ))?)\n872\t}\n873\t\n874\t/// Build an error response as JSON (for forwarded node errors).\n875\tfn build_json_error_response(resp: DocumentsWriteResponse) -> Response {\n876\t    (\n877\t        StatusCode::OK,\n878\t        [(header::CONTENT_TYPE, \"application/json\")],\n879\t        Json(resp),\n880\t    )\n881\t        .into_response()\n882\t}\n883\t\n884\t#[cfg(test)]\n885\tmod tests {\n886\t    use super::*;\n887\t    use miroir_core::api_error::{MiroirCode, Implements P2.2 write path:\n//! - Primary key extraction on the hot path\n//! - `_miroir_shard` injection\n//! - Reserved field rejection\n//! - Two-rule quorum\n//!\n//! Implements P2.5 task reconciliation:\n//! - Collects per-node task UIDs\n//! - Registers Miroir task ID (mtask-<uuid>)\n//! - Returns mtask ID to client\n//!\n//! Implements §13.6 session pinning:\n//! - Records writes with session header\n//! - Tracks pinned group (first to reach quorum)\n\nuse axum::extract::{Extension, Path, Query};\nuse \"Option::is_none\")]\n    #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n    error_type: Option<String>,\n}\n\n/// Response for write operations.\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct DocumentsWriteResponse {\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    taskUid: Option<String>, // Changed to String to hold mtask-<uuid>\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    indexUid: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    status: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    error: Option<String>,\n \"X-Miroir-Degraded\";\n\n/// Quorum tracking state for write operations.\n#[derive(Debug, Default)]\nstruct QuorumState {\n    /// Per-group ACK counts: group_id -> successful_ack_count\n    group_acks: HashMap<u32, usize>,\n    /// Per-group total node counts: group_id -> total_nodes_attempted\n    group_totals: HashMap<u32, usize>,\n    /// Groups that met quorum: group_id -> true\n    groups_met_quorum: HashMap<u32, bool>,\n    /// Total degraded groups count\n    degraded_groups: u32,\n}\n\nimpl QuorumState {\n    /// Record a write attempt to a node.\n    fn record_attempt(&mut self, group_id: u32, _node_id: &NodeId) {\n        *self.group_totals.entry(group_id).or_insert(0) += 1;\n    }\n\n    /// Record a successful write ACK from a node.\n    fn record_success(&mut self, group_id: u32, _node_id: &NodeId) {\n        *self.group_acks.entry(group_id).or_insert(0) += 1;\n    }\n\n    /// Record a failed write attempt from a node.\n    fn record_failure(&mut self, _group_id: u32) {\n        // Track that this group had a failure\n        // Degraded is determined after checking quorum\n    }\n\n    /// Check if a group has met quorum: floor(RF/2) + 1 ACKs required.\n    fn check_group_quorum(&mut self, group_id: u32, rf: usize) -> bool {\n        let acks = *self.group_acks.get(&group_id).unwrap_or(&0);\n        let quorum = (rf / 2) + 1;\n        let met = acks >= quorum;\n        *self.groups_met_quorum.entry(group_id).or_insert(false) = met;\n        met\n    }\n\n    /// Count how many groups met quorum.\n    fn count_quorum_groups(&self) -> usize {\n        self.groups_met_quorum.values().filter(|&&v| v).count()\n    }\n\n    /// Count degraded groups (groups that exist but didn't meet quorum).\n    fn count_degraded_groups(&mut self, replica_group_count: u32, rf: usize) -> u32 {\n        let mut degraded = 0u32;\n        for group_id in 0..replica_group_count {\n            if !self.check_group_quorum(group_id, rf) {\n                // Only count as degraded if we attempted to write to this group\n                if self.group_totals.contains_key(&group_id) {\n                    degraded += 1;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        degraded\n    }\n}\n\n/// Build router for document endpoints.\npub fn router<S>() -> Router<S>\nwhere\n    S: Clone + Send + Sync + 'static,\n{\n    Router::new()\n        .route(\"/\", axum::routing::post(post_documents))\n        .route(\"/\", axum::routing::put(put_documents))\n        .route(\"/\", axum::routing::delete(delete_documents))\n        .route(\"/:id\", session_id.and_then(|ext| {\n        let s = ext.0;\n        if s.0.is_empty() { None } else { Some(s.0.clone()) }\n    });\n\n    write_documents_impl(index, params.primaryKey, documents, &state, sid).await\n}\n\n/// PUT /indexes/{uid}/documents - Replace documents.\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %index))]\nasync fn put_documents(\n    Path(index): Path<String>,\n    Query(params): write_documents_impl(index, params.primaryKey, documents, &state, sid).await\n}\n\n/// DELETE /indexes/{uid}/documents - Delete by IDs or filter.\nasync fn delete_documents(\n    Path(index): MeilisearchError> {\n    let sid = session_id.and_then(|ext| {\n        let s = ext.0;\n        if s.0.is_empty() { None } else { Some(s.0.clone()) }\n    });\n\n    // Try to parse as delete by origin: None, // Client write\n        };\n        return delete_by_filter_impl(index, req, &state, sid).await;\n    }\n\n    // Try to parse as delete by IDs\n    if let Some(ids) = body.get(\"ids\").and_then(|v| v.as_array()) {\n        let ids: Vec<String> = ids\n            .iter()\n            .filter_map(|v| v.as_str().map(|s| s.to_string()))\n            .collect();\n        if !ids.is_empty() {\n            let req = DeleteByIdsRequest {\n                index_uid: index.clone(),\n                ids,\n                origin: None, // Client write\n            };\n            return delete_by_ids_impl(index, req, &state, sid).await;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we get here, the request body is malformed\n    Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n        MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n        \"delete request must include either 'filter' or 'ids' field\",\n    ))\n}\n\n/// DELETE /indexes/{uid}/documents/{id} - Delete single document by ID.\nasync fn delete_document_by_id(\n    Path((index, id)): Path<(String, String)>,\n    Extension(state): Extension<Arc<AppState>>,\n    session_id: Option<Extension<crate::middleware::SessionId>>,\n) -> Implementation for write documents (POST/PUT).\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %index, session_id))]\nasync fn write_documents_impl(\n    index: String,\n    primary_key: Option<String>,\n    mut documents: Vec<Value>,\n    state: &AppState,\n    session_id: Option<String>,\n) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n    if documents.is_empty() {\n        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n            \"cannot write empty document batch\",\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // 1. Resolve alias to concrete index UID (plan §13.7)\n    // Aliases are resolved before any processing; writes to multi-target aliases are rejected\n    let index_uid = if state.config.aliases.enabled {\n        // Check if the index is an alias\n        let resolved = state.alias_registry.resolve(&index).await;\n        if resolved != vec![index.clone()] {\n            // It was an alias\n            // Check if it's a multi-target alias (read-only, ILM-managed)\n            if state.alias_registry.is_multi_target_alias(&index).await {\n                return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                    MiroirCode::MultiAliasNotWritable,\n                    format!(\n                        \"alias '{}' is a multi-target alias and is read-only (managed by ILM); writes must go to the concrete index or the write alias\",\n                        index\n                    ),\n                ));\n            }\n            // Single-target alias: record resolution metric and use the target\n            state.metrics.inc_alias_resolution(&index);\n            resolved.into_iter().next().unwrap_or_else(|| index.clone())\n        } else {\n            // Not an alias, use the index name as-is\n            index.clone()\n        }\n    } else {\n        index.clone()\n    };\n\n    // 1. Extract primary key from first document if not provided\n    let primary_key = primary_key.or_else(|| {\n        documents\n            .first()\n            .and_then(|doc| extract_primary_key(doc))\n    });\n\n    let primary_key = primary_key.ok_or_else(|| {\n        MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n            format!(\"primary key required for index `{}`\", index),\n        )\n    })?;\n\n    // 2. Validate all documents have the primary key and check for reserved field\n    let anti_entropy_enabled = state.config.anti_entropy.enabled;\n    let updated_at_field = &state.config.anti_entropy.updated_at_field;\n    let ttl_enabled = state.config.ttl.enabled;\n    let expires_at_field = &state.config.ttl.expires_at_field;\n\n    for (i, doc) in documents.iter().enumerate() {\n        // Check for reserved field BEFORE checking primary key (per acceptance criteria)\n        // _miroir_shard is ALWAYS reserved (plan §5)\n        if doc.get(\"_miroir_shard\").is_some() {\n            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n                \"document contains reserved field `_miroir_shard`\",\n            ));\n        }\n\n        // _miroir_updated_at is reserved ONLY when anti_entropy.enabled: true (plan §5, §13.8)\n        if anti_entropy_enabled && doc.get(updated_at_field).is_some() {\n            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n                format!(\"document contains reserved field `{}` (reserved when anti_entropy.enabled: true)\", updated_at_field),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        // _miroir_expires_at is reserved ONLY when ttl.enabled: true (plan §5, §13.14)\n        // When reserved, clients cannot SET it; the orchestrator controls it. When disabled,\n        // client values pass through end-to-end.\n        if ttl_enabled && doc.get(expires_at_field).is_some() {\n            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n                format!(\"document contains reserved field `{}` (reserved when ttl.enabled: true)\", expires_at_field),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        if doc.get(&primary_key).is_none() {\n            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n                format!(\n                    \"document at index {} missing primary key field `{}`\",\n                    i, primary_key\n                ),\n            ));\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Inject _miroir_shard and _miroir_updated_at into each document\n    let topology = state.topology.read().await;\n    let shard_count = topology.shards;\n    let rf = topology.rf();\n    let replica_group_count = topology.replica_group_count();\n\n    // Get current timestamp in milliseconds since epoch for _miroir_updated_at stamping\n    let now_ms = if anti_entropy_enabled {\n        Some(\n            std::time::SystemTime::now()\n                .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)\n                .unwrap_or_default()\n                .as_millis() as u64\n        )\n    } else {\n        None\n    };\n\n    for doc in &mut documents {\n        if let Some(pk_value) = doc.get(&primary_key).and_then(|v| v.as_str()) {\n            let shard_id = shard_for_key(pk_value, shard_count);\n            doc[\"_miroir_shard\"] = serde_json::json!(shard_id);\n        }\n\n        // Stamp _miroir_updated_at when anti_entropy is enabled (plan §13.8)\n        // This happens AFTER reserved field validation, so orchestrator-controlled injection is allowed\n        if let Some(timestamp) = now_ms {\n            doc[updated_at_field] = serde_json::json!(timestamp);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 4. Group documents by target nodes (per-batch grouping for efficient fan-out)\n    let node_documents = group_documents_by_shard(&documents, &primary_key, &topology)?;\n\n    // 5. Fan out to nodes and track quorum\n    let client = HttpClient::new(\n        state.config.node_master_key.clone(),\n        state.config.scatter.node_timeout_ms,\n    );\n\n    let mut quorum_state = QuorumState::default();\n    let mut node_task_uids: HashMap<String, u64> = HashMap::new();\n\n    // For each shard, write to all RF nodes in each replica group (with dual-write support)\n    for (shard_id, docs) in node_documents {\n        // Get migration coordinator reference for dual-write detection\n        let migration_coordinator = state.migration_coordinator.as_ref().map(|c| {\n            // We need a read lock on the coordinator\n            tokio::task::block_in_place(|| {\n                tokio::runtime::Handle::current().block_on(async {\n                    c.read().await\n                })\n            })\n        });\n\n        // Use migration-aware routing\n        let targets = write_targets_with_migration(\n            shard_id,\n            &topology,\n            migration_coordinator.as_deref(),\n        );\n\n        if targets.is_empty() {\n            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n                format!(\"no available nodes for shard {}\", shard_id),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        // Track which groups we're targeting for this shard\n\n        for node_id in targets {\n            let node = topology\n                .node(&node_id)\n                .ok_or_else(|| MeilisearchError::new(MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable, \"node not found in topology\"))?;\n\n            let group_id = node.replica_group;\n            quorum_state.record_attempt(group_id, &node_id);\n\n            let req = WriteRequest {\n                index_uid: index_uid.clone(),\n                documents: docs.clone(),\n                primary_key: Some(primary_key.clone()),\n                origin: None, // Client write\n            };\n\n            match client.write_documents(&node_id, &node.address, &req).await {\n                Ok(resp) if resp.success => {\n                    quorum_state.record_success(group_id, &node_id);\n                    if let Some(task_uid) = resp.task_uid {\n                        node_task_uids.insert(node_id.as_str().to_string(), task_uid);\n                    }\n                }\n                Ok(resp) => {\n                    // Non-success response (validation error, etc.)\n                    return Ok(build_json_error_response(build_error_response(resp)));\n                }\n                Err(_) => {\n                    quorum_state.record_failure(group_id);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 6. Apply two-rule quorum logic\n    let degraded_groups = quorum_state.count_degraded_groups(replica_group_count, rf);\n    let quorum_groups = quorum_state.count_quorum_groups();\n\n    // Write success if at least one group met quorum\n    if quorum_groups == 0 {\n        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::NoQuorum,\n            \"no replica group met quorum\",\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // 6.5. Find the first group to reach quorum (for session pinning, plan §13.6)\n    // Groups are checked in ascending order, so the first one with quorum is the first\n    let first_quorum_group = (0..replica_group_count)\n        .find(|&group_id| {\n            let acks = *quorum_state.group_acks.get(&group_id).unwrap_or(&0);\n            let quorum = (rf / 2) + 1;\n            acks >= quorum\n        })\n        .unwrap_or(0); // Default to group 0 if somehow no quorum (shouldn't happen here)\n\n    // 7. Register Miroir task with collected node task UIDs\n    let miroir_task = state\n        .task_registry\n        .register_with_metadata(\n            node_task_uids.clone(),\n            Some(index_uid.clone()),\n            Some(\"documentAdditionOrUpdate\".to_string()),\n        )\n        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n            format!(\"failed to register task: {}\", e),\n        ))?;\n\n    // 7.5. Record session pinning if session header present (plan §13.6)\n    if let (Some(ref sid), true) = (&session_id, state.session_manager.is_enabled()) {\n        if let Err(e) = state.session_manager.record_write_with_quorum(\n            sid,\n            miroir_task.miroir_id.clone(),\n            first_quorum_group,\n        ).await {\n            // Log error but don't fail the write - session pinning is best-effort\n            tracing::error!(\n                session_id = %sid,\n                error = %e,\n                \"failed to record session pinning for write\"\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Build success response with degraded header and mtask ID\n    build_response_with_degraded_header(\n        DocumentsWriteResponse {\n            taskUid: Some(miroir_task.miroir_id),\n            indexUid: Some(index_uid.clone()),\n            status: Some(\"enqueued\".to_string()),\n            error: None,\n            error_type: None,\n            code: None,\n            link: None,\n        },\n        degraded_groups,\n    )\n}\n\n/// Implementation for delete by IDs.\nasync fn delete_by_ids_impl(\n    index: String,\n    req: DeleteByIdsRequest,\n    state: &AppState,\n    session_id: Option<String>,\n) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n    if req.ids.is_empty() {\n        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n            \"cannot delete empty ID list\",\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Resolve alias to concrete index UID (plan §13.7)\n    let index_uid = if state.config.aliases.enabled {\n        let resolved = state.alias_registry.resolve(&index).await;\n        if resolved != vec![index.clone()] {\n            // It was an alias - check if it's a multi-target alias (read-only)\n            if state.alias_registry.is_multi_target_alias(&index).await {\n                return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                    MiroirCode::MultiAliasNotWritable,\n                    format!(\n                        \"alias '{}' is a multi-target alias and is read-only (managed by ILM); deletes must go to the concrete index or the write alias\",\n                        index\n                    ),\n                ));\n            }\n            // Single-target alias: record resolution metric and use the target\n            state.metrics.inc_alias_resolution(&index);\n            resolved.into_iter().next().unwrap_or_else(|| index.clone())\n        } else {\n            index.clone()\n        }\n    } else {\n        index.clone()\n    };\n\n    let topology = state.topology.read().await;\n    let rf = topology.rf();\n    let replica_group_count = topology.replica_group_count();\n\n    // Group IDs by target shard for independent per-shard routing\n    let mut shard_ids: HashMap<u32, Vec<String>> = HashMap::new();\n    for id in &req.ids {\n        let shard_id = shard_for_key(id, topology.shards);\n        shard_ids.entry(shard_id).or_default().push(id.clone());\n    }\n\n    let client = HttpClient::new(\n        state.config.node_master_key.clone(),\n        state.config.scatter.node_timeout_ms,\n    );\n\n    let mut quorum_state = QuorumState::default();\n    let mut node_task_uids: HashMap<String, u64> = HashMap::new();\n\n    // For each shard, write to all RF nodes in each replica group\n    for (shard_id, ids) in shard_ids {\n        let targets = miroir_core::router::write_targets(shard_id, &topology);\n\n        if targets.is_empty() {\n            return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n                MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n                format!(\"no available nodes for shard {}\", shard_id),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        for node_id in targets {\n            let node = topology\n                .node(&node_id)\n                .ok_or_else(|| MeilisearchError::new(MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable, \"node not found in topology\"))?;\n\n            let group_id = node.replica_group;\n            quorum_state.record_attempt(group_id, &node_id);\n\n            let delete_req = DeleteByIdsRequest {\n                index_uid: index_uid.clone(),\n                ids: ids.clone(),\n                origin: None, // Client write\n            };\n\n            match client.delete_documents(&node_id, &node.address, &delete_req).await {\n                Ok(resp) if resp.success => {\n                    quorum_state.record_success(group_id, &node_id);\n                    if let Some(task_uid) = resp.task_uid {\n                        node_task_uids.insert(node_id.as_str().to_string(), task_uid);\n                    }\n                }\n                Ok(resp) => {\n                    return Ok(build_json_error_response(build_error_response(resp)));\n                }\n                Err(_) => {\n                    quorum_state.record_failure(group_id);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Apply two-rule quorum logic\n    let degraded_groups = quorum_state.count_degraded_groups(replica_group_count, rf);\n    let quorum_groups = quorum_state.count_quorum_groups();\n\n    // Write success if at least one group met quorum\n    if quorum_groups == 0 {\n        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::NoQuorum,\n            \"no replica group met quorum\",\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Find the first group to reach quorum (for session pinning, plan §13.6)\n    let first_quorum_group = (0..replica_group_count)\n        .find(|&group_id| {\n            let acks = *quorum_state.group_acks.get(&group_id).unwrap_or(&0);\n            let quorum = (rf / 2) + 1;\n            acks >= quorum\n        })\n        .unwrap_or(0);\n\n    // Register Miroir task with collected node task UIDs\n    let miroir_task = state\n        .task_registry\n        .register_with_metadata(\n            node_task_uids.clone(),\n            Some(index.clone()),\n            Some(\"documentDeletion\".to_string()),\n        )\n        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n            format!(\"failed to register task: {}\", e),\n        ))?;\n\n    // Record session pinning if session header present (plan §13.6)\n    if let (Some(ref sid), true) = (&session_id, state.session_manager.is_enabled()) {\n        if let Err(e) = state.session_manager.record_write_with_quorum(\n            sid,\n            miroir_task.miroir_id.clone(),\n            first_quorum_group,\n        ).await {\n            tracing::error!(\n                session_id = %sid,\n                error = %e,\n                \"failed to record session pinning for delete\"\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    build_response_with_degraded_header(\n        DocumentsWriteResponse {\n            taskUid: Some(miroir_task.miroir_id),\n            indexUid: Some(index.clone()),\n            status: Some(\"enqueued\".to_string()),\n            error: None,\n            error_type: None,\n            code: None,\n            link: None,\n        },\n        degraded_groups,\n    )\n}\n\n/// Implementation for delete by filter (broadcast to all nodes).\nasync fn delete_by_filter_impl(\n    index: String,\n    req: DeleteByFilterRequest,\n    state: &AppState,\n    session_id: Option<String>,\n) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n    let topology = state.topology.read().await;\n    let rf = topology.rf();\n    let replica_group_count = topology.replica_group_count();\n\n    let client = HttpClient::new(\n        state.config.node_master_key.clone(),\n        state.config.scatter.node_timeout_ms,\n    );\n\n    let mut quorum_state = QuorumState::default();\n    let mut node_task_uids: HashMap<String, u64> = HashMap::new();\n\n    // Broadcast to all nodes (cannot shard-route for filters)\n    for node in topology.nodes() {\n        let group_id = node.replica_group;\n        quorum_state.record_attempt(group_id, &node.id);\n\n        match client\n            .delete_documents_by_filter(&node.id, &node.address, &req)\n            .await\n        {\n            Ok(resp) if resp.success => {\n                quorum_state.record_success(group_id, &node.id);\n                if let Some(task_uid) = resp.task_uid {\n                    node_task_uids.insert(node.id.as_str().to_string(), task_uid);\n                }\n            }\n            Ok(resp) => {\n                return Ok(build_json_error_response(build_error_response(resp)));\n            }\n            Err(_) => {\n                quorum_state.record_failure(group_id);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Apply two-rule quorum logic\n    let degraded_groups = quorum_state.count_degraded_groups(replica_group_count, rf);\n    let quorum_groups = quorum_state.count_quorum_groups();\n\n    // Write success if at least one group met quorum\n    if quorum_groups == 0 {\n        return Err(MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::NoQuorum,\n            \"no replica group met quorum\",\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Find the first group to reach quorum (for session pinning, plan §13.6)\n    let first_quorum_group = (0..replica_group_count)\n        .find(|&group_id| {\n            let acks = *quorum_state.group_acks.get(&group_id).unwrap_or(&0);\n            let quorum = (rf / 2) + 1;\n            acks >= quorum\n        })\n        .unwrap_or(0);\n\n    // Register Miroir task with collected node task UIDs\n    let miroir_task = state\n        .task_registry\n        .register_with_metadata(\n            node_task_uids.clone(),\n            Some(index.clone()),\n            Some(\"documentDeletion\".to_string()),\n        )\n        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n            format!(\"failed to register task: {}\", e),\n        ))?;\n\n    // Record session pinning if session header present (plan §13.6)\n    if let (Some(ref sid), true) = (&session_id, state.session_manager.is_enabled()) {\n        if let Err(e) = state.session_manager.record_write_with_quorum(\n            sid,\n            miroir_task.miroir_id.clone(),\n            first_quorum_group,\n        ).await {\n            tracing::error!(\n                session_id = %sid,\n                error = %e,\n                \"failed to record session pinning for delete by filter\"\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    build_response_with_degraded_header(\n        DocumentsWriteResponse {\n            taskUid: Some(miroir_task.miroir_id),\n            indexUid: Some(index.clone()),\n            status: Some(\"enqueued\".to_string()),\n            error: None,\n            error_type: None,\n            code: None,\n            link: None,\n        },\n        degraded_groups,\n    )\n}\n\n/// Extract primary key from a document by checking common field names.\n///\n/// Tries fields in order: id, pk, key, _id.\nfn extract_primary_key(doc: &Value) -> Option<String> {\n    [\"id\", \"pk\", \"key\", \"_id\"]\n        .iter()\n        .find(|&&key| doc.get(key).is_some())\n        .map(|&s| s.to_string())\n}\n\n/// Group documents by their target shard for fan-out optimization.\n///\n/// Returns a map of shard_id -> documents to send to that shard.\n/// The caller then fans out each shard's documents to all RF nodes in each group.\n///\n/// This per-batch grouping minimizes HTTP fan-out count (critical at scale).\nfn group_documents_by_shard(\n    documents: &[Value],\n    primary_key: &str,\n    topology: &Topology,\n) -> std::result::Result<HashMap<u32, Vec<Value>>, MeilisearchError> {\n    let mut shard_documents: HashMap<u32, Vec<Value>> = HashMap::new();\n\n    for doc in documents {\n        let pk_value = doc\n            .get(primary_key)\n            .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n            .ok_or_else(|| {\n                MeilisearchError::new(\n                    MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n                    \"primary key value must be a string\",\n                )\n            })?;\n\n        let shard_id = shard_for_key(pk_value, topology.shards);\n        shard_documents\n            .entry(shard_id)\n            .or_default()\n            .push(doc.clone());\n    }\n\n    Ok(shard_documents)\n}\n\n/// Build an error response from a node error.\nfn build_error_response(resp: WriteResponse) -> DocumentsWriteResponse {\n    DocumentsWriteResponse {\n        taskUid: resp.task_uid.map(|uid| uid.to_string()),\n        indexUid: None,\n        status: None,\n        error: resp.message,\n        error_type: resp.error_type,\n        code: resp.code,\n        link: None,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Build a success response with optional X-Miroir-Degraded header.\nfn build_response_with_degraded_header(\n    response: DocumentsWriteResponse,\n    degraded_groups: u32,\n) -> std::result::Result<Response, MeilisearchError> {\n    let body = serde_json::to_string(&response).map_err(|e| {\n        MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n            format!(\"failed to serialize response: {}\", e),\n        )\n    })?;\n\n    let mut builder = Response::builder()\n        .status(StatusCode::OK)\n        .header(header::CONTENT_TYPE, \"application/json\");\n\n    // Add X-Miroir-Degraded header if any groups were degraded\n    if degraded_groups > 0 {\n        builder = builder.header(HEADER_MIROIR_DEGRADED, format!(\"groups={}\", degraded_groups));\n    }\n\n    Ok(builder\n        .body(axum::body::Body::from(body))\n        .map_err(|e| MeilisearchError::new(\n            MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n            format!(\"failed to build response: {}\", e),\n        ))?)\n}\n\n/// Build an error response as JSON (for forwarded node errors).\nfn build_json_error_response(resp: DocumentsWriteResponse) -> Response {\n    (\n        StatusCode::OK,\n        [(header::CONTENT_TYPE, \"application/json\")],\n        Json(resp),\n    )\n        .into_response()\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use miroir_core::api_error::{MiroirCode, MeilisearchError};\n    use serde_json::json;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn
